{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01WeuHEsH4pgwPGaCU1QBszd","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I see the issue more clearly. Looking at the code in `braveadblock.py`:\n\n```python\ndef read_cache(self) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Initialize the adblocking engine from cache file.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        cache_exists = self._cache_path.is_file()\n    except OSError:\n        logger.error(\"Failed to read adblock cache\", exc_info=True)\n        return\n\n    if cache_exists:\n        logger.debug(\"Loading cached adblock data: %s\", self._cache_path)\n        try:\n            with _map_exceptions():\n                self._engine.deserialize_from_file(str(self._cache_path))\n        except DeserializationError as e:\n            message.error(\"Reading adblock filter data failed (corrupted data?). \"\n                          \"Please run :adblock-update.\")\n```\n\nThere's a test already in `test_braveadblock.py` at line 423-432 called `test_corrupt_cache_handling`. It checks that when a corrupted cache is loaded, an error message is shown.\n\nHowever, looking at the description of the task, it says:\n> When qutebrowser starts up and attempts to load the ad-blocker filter cache, the application crashes if the cache file is corrupted or contains invalid data.\n\nThe test exists at line 423-432 and it seems like it's already written to test this behavior. But the task is to write a regression test that demonstrates the bug.\n\nLet me look more carefully at the code flow:\n\n1. In `braveadblock.py` line 347, when the module is initialized via `init()`, it calls `ad_blocker.read_cache()`\n2. The `read_cache()` method at line 239-262 tries to deserialize the cache file\n3. The exception handling in the\nread_cache() method should catch deserialization errors and show an error\nmessage, but in the current buggy code, exceptions are not properly caught.\n\nThe issue is in the _map_exceptions() context manager and the exception\nhandling in read_cache():\n- _map_exceptions() only catches specific exception types\n- If the adblock library raises an exception that's not properly mapped,\n  it propagates as an unhandled exception\n- This causes the application to crash during initialization before the\n  browser window even appears\n\nExpected Behavior:\n- Corrupted cache files should be detected\n- An error message should be shown to the user\n- The application should continue running normally\n- The user can browse without ad blocking until the cache is rebuilt\n\"\"\"\n\nimport pathlib\nimport logging\nimport tempfile\nimport sys\nfrom unittest import mock\n\n# Set up path for imports\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\n# Import after path modification - this must be before pytest.importorskip\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QObject, pyqtSignal, pyqtSlot\nfrom qutebrowser.utils import usertypes, message\nfrom qutebrowser.components import braveadblock\n\n# Skip if adblock is not available\npytest.importorskip(\"adblock\")\n\n\nclass TestAdblockCacheCorruptionRegression:\n    \"\"\"Regression test for adblock cache corruption crash bug.\n\n    The bug causes the application to crash when loading a corrupted cache\n    file.
